  $ pacman -Syu

 Error will occur, ignore it and reboot machine to be save:

      0 [main] pacman (5420) C:\msys64\usr\bin\pacman.exe: *** fatal error - cygheap base mismatch detected - 0x18034B408/0x180352408.

Warning: Use with caution. Disabling package signing will allow pacman to install untrusted packages automatically.
If you are not concerned about package signing, you can disable PGP signature checking completely. Edit /etc/pacman.conf and uncomment>

$ pacman -Syu

This shall complete without errors.

$  nano /etc/pacman.conf
Comment:
SigLevel    = Required
Uncomment:
